ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span

(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p

fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;
line-height:normal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-

language:DE">Treffpunkt: Bootshaus des Regensburger Ruderklubs,

style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;
line-height:normal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures: none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-

New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Treffpunkt: Bootshaus des Regensburger Ruderklubs,
Messerschmittstraße 2    <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New

Tabelle";         mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;         mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;

top:0cm;         mso-para-margin-right:0cm;         mso-para-margin-
bottom:8.0pt;         mso-para-margin-left:0cm;         line-height:107%;
mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-
family:"Aptos",sans-serif;         mso-ascii-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-hansi-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;         mso-
ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-

fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-

language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern

mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern

Tabelle";         mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;         mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;
mso-style-noshow:yes;         mso-style-priority:99;         mso-style-
parent:"";         mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;         mso-para-margin-
top:0cm;         mso-para-margin-right:0cm;         mso-para-margin-
bottom:8.0pt;         mso-para-margin-left:0cm;         line-height:107%;
mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-
family:"Aptos",sans-serif;         mso-ascii-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-hansi-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;         mso-
ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span

parent:"";         mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;         mso-para-margin-
top:0cm;         mso-para-margin-right:0cm;         mso-para-margin-
bottom:8.0pt;         mso-para-margin-left:0cm;         line-height:107%;
mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-

ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-hansi-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;         mso-
ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie

Tabelle";         mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;         mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;

parent:"";         mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;         mso-para-margin-
top:0cm;         mso-para-margin-right:0cm;         mso-para-margin-
bottom:8.0pt;         mso-para-margin-left:0cm;         line-height:107%;
mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-
family:"Aptos",sans-serif;         mso-ascii-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-hansi-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;         mso-
ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;
line-height:normal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures: none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;

ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;

family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-

language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-

language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span

fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-

die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:

fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-

Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-

fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:

(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-

fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-

fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:

(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-

family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Erlernen der Grundlagen
der Rudertechnik; je nach Temperatur, Wind und Pegelstand ungefähr die erste
Hälfte des Semesters als Mannschaft im Doppelvierer und die zweite im Einer
(Rennbootform).  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst"
style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto; text-indent:-18.0pt;line-
height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-
fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span

family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo1"><span

fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-

family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Erlernen und Verbesserung der Rudertechnik, Erhöhung der Sicherheit
beim Steuern des Bootes (bevorzugt im Einer). Ziel ist das selbstständige,
verkehrssichere, materialschonende Rudern gemäß der Ruder- und Fahrtordnung.
<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;

fareast-language:DE">sicheres Großbootfahren  <p

auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span

Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-

language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span

fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span

(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-

Tabelle";         mso-tstyle-rowband-size:0;         mso-tstyle-colband-size:0;
mso-style-noshow:yes;         mso-style-priority:99;         mso-style-
parent:"";         mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;         mso-para-margin-
top:0cm;         mso-para-margin-right:0cm;         mso-para-margin-
bottom:8.0pt;         mso-para-margin-left:0cm;         line-height:107%;
mso-pagination:widow-orphan;         font-size:11.0pt;         font-
family:"Aptos",sans-serif;         mso-ascii-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
ascii-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-hansi-font-family:Aptos;         mso-
hansi-theme-font:minor-latin;         mso-font-kerning:1.0pt;         mso-
ligatures:standardcontextual;         mso-fareast-language:EN-US;}    <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Rudern auf Donau und Naab<span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">   <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-
fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Beim Rudern im Hochschulsport könnt ihr
die gängigen Bootsmanöver, die Mannschaftskoordination im stabilen Doppelvierer
sowie das Steuern und die Balance im schmalen Einer lernen.   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">&nbsp;<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">   <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Erlernen und Verbesserung der Rudertechnik, Erhöhung der Sicherheit
beim Steuern des Bootes (bevorzugt im Einer). Ziel ist das selbstständige,
verkehrssichere, materialschonende Rudern gemäß der Ruder- und Fahrtordnung.
<span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-family:&quot;Times New
Roman&quot;,serif;mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-
kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-language:DE">Voraussetzungen:  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;
text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo2"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sicheres Großbootfahren  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">ausreichende Schwimmfähigkeit ("Freischwimmer" bzw.
Bronzeabzeichen)  <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">keine gesundheitlichen Bedenken gegen die Sportart Rudern
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:
auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span
style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family:
Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">Empfehlung des Abschließens einer Haftpflichtversicherung
(falls nicht vorhanden)   <p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin-
bottom:0cm;mso-add-space: auto;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:normal;mso-
list:l1 level1 lfo1"><span style="font-family:Symbol;mso-fareast-font-
family:Symbol;mso-bidi-font-family: Symbol;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures:none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">·&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; <span
style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-
fareast-language:DE">sorgfältige Lektüre der Fahrtordnung und Revierinfos sowie
die Abgabe der unterschriebenen <span style="color:#4C94D8;mso-themecolor:
text2;mso-themetint:128">Ruder-Bestätigung bei der Kursleitung  <p
class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin-bottom:0cm;mso-add-space:auto;
line-height:normal"><span style="font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif;
mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-
ligatures: none;mso-fareast-language:DE">&nbsp;  <span style="font-
family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;,serif; mso-fareast-font-family:&quot;Times
New Roman&quot;;mso-font-kerning:0pt;mso-ligatures: none;mso-fareast-
language:DE">Treffpunkt: Bootshaus des Regensburger Ruderklubs,
Messerschmittstraße 2

</Locale>
<Locale value="en">
 

 Rowing on the Danube and Naab: When rowing in university sports, you can learn
the common boat maneuvers, team coordination in a stable double four, as well as
steering and balance in a narrow single. Participation is only possible for
experienced swimmers / free swimmers and only if there are no health concerns
about the sport of rowing. All course participants (including free rowing) are
recommended to take out liability insurance. Beginners' course: Learning the
basics of rowing technique; depending on the temperature, wind and water level,
approximately the first half of the semester as a team in a double four and the
second in a single (racing boat form). Meeting point: Boathouse of the
Regensburg Rowing Club, Messerschmittstrasse 2

 Rowing on the Danube and Naab: When rowing in university sports, you can learn
the common boat maneuvers, team coordination in a stable double four, and
steering and balance in a narrow single. Participation is only possible for
experienced swimmers/free swimmers and only if there are no health concerns
about the sport of rowing. All course participants (including free rowing) are
recommended to take out liability insurance. Advanced course: Learning and
improving rowing technique, increasing safety when steering the boat (preferably
in a single). The goal is independent, roadworthy, material-friendly rowing in
accordance with the rowing and driving regulations. Requirements: Safe driving
of large boats, submission of the completed and signed rowing confirmation to
the course leader and knowledge of the driving regulations. Meeting point:
Boathouse of the Regensburg Rowing Club, Messerschmittstrasse 2

recommended to take out liability insurance. Advanced course: Learning and
improving rowing technique, increasing safety when steering the boat (preferably
in a single). The goal is independent, roadworthy, material-friendly rowing in
accordance with the rowing and driving regulations. Requirements: Safe driving
of large boats, submission of the completed and signed rowing confirmation to
the course leader and knowledge of the driving regulations. Meeting point:
Boathouse of the Regensburg Rowing Club, Messerschmittstrasse 2
